<h2 class="kt-adv-heading81208_86a0ce-d6 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading81208_86a0ce-d6">Meet  <strong>Emma</strong></h2>



<p>Hello! I&#8217;m Emma Russo, a passionate 35-year-old chef hailing from San Francisco,  My culinary creations are inspired by the vibrant flavors of fresh citrus, aromatic herbs, the refreshing sea breeze, and the comforting richness of beans—ingredients that remind me of home.<br></p>
